
---- TRUNCATE TABLE 명령으로 모든 테이블 삭제
DO $$
DECLARE
    table_name text;
BEGIN
    FOR table_name IN
        SELECT tablename
        FROM pg_tables
        WHERE schemaname = 'plant_i'
    LOOP
        EXECUTE format('TRUNCATE TABLE %I RESTART IDENTITY CASCADE', table_name);
    END LOOP;
END $$;
